               ast.Mod: operator.mod\n                }\n                for op_type, fn in ops.items():\n                    if isinstance(op, op_type):\n                        return fn(left,                         "import unittest\nfrom unittest.mock import patch, MagicMock, mock_open\nimport tempfile\nimport os\n\n# Import the code to test\n# Since Django models/forms/views require a Django environment, we focus on utility functions and formula evaluation logic.\n# We'll test:\n# - main_app/utils.py: extract_text, summarize_text\n# - main_app/views.py: formula evaluation logic (SafeEval)\n\n# For formula evaluation, we'll extract the SafeEval logic into a testable class.\n# For extract_text, we'll mock file reads and docx/PyPDF2.\n\n# --- Begin: Code under test (extracted for testing purposes) ---\n\nimport ast\nimport operator\n\ndef get_safe_eval_class():\n    import math\n    allowed_names = {\n        'abs': abs,\n        'max': max,\n        'min': min,\n        'pow': pow\n    }\n    allowed_names.update({k: getattr(math, k) for k in dir(math) if not k.startswith(\"_\")})\n\n    class SafeEval(ast.NodeVisitor):\n        def __init__(self, values):\n            self.values = values\n\n        def visit(self, node):\n            if isinstance(node, ast.Expression):\n                return self.visit(node.body)\n            elif isinstance(node, ast.BinOp):\n                left = self.visit(node.left)\n                right = self.visit(node.right)\n                return self._binop(node.op, left, right)\n            elif isinstance(node, ast.UnaryOp):\n                operand = self.visit(node.operand)\n                return self._unaryop(node.op, operand)\n            elif isinstance(node, ast.Call):\n                func = self.visit(node.func)\n                args = [self.visit(a) for a in node.args]\n                if func in allowed_names:\n                    return allowed_names[func](*args)\n                else:\n                    raise ValueError(\"Unsafe function call\")\n            elif isinstance(node, ast.Name):\n                if node.id in self.values:\n                    return self.values[node.id]\n                elif node.id in allowed_names:\n                    return node.id\n                else:\n                    raise ValueError(f\"Unknown variable: {node.id}\")\n            elif isinstance(node, ast.Num):\n                return node.n\n            elif isinstance(node, ast.Constant):\n                return node.value\n            else:\n                raise ValueError(\"Unsafe expression\")\n        def _binop(self, op, left, right):\n            ops = {\n                ast.Add: operator.add,\n                ast.Sub: operator.sub,\n                ast.Mult: operator.mul,\n                ast.Div: operator.truediv,\n                ast.Pow: operator.pow,\n                ast.Mod: operator.mod\n            }\n            for op_type, fn in ops.items():\n                if isinstance(op, op_type):\n                    return fn(left, right)\n            raise ValueError(\"Unsupported operator\")\n        def _unaryop(self, op, operand):\n            if isinstance(op, ast.USub):\n                return -operand\n            elif isinstance(op, ast.UAdd):\n                return +operand\n            else:\n                raise ValueError(\"Unsupported unary operator\")\n    return SafeEval\n\n# --- End: Code under test ---\n\n# Now, import extract_text and summarize_text from main_app/utils.py\n# We'll simulate/mock their dependencies.\n\n# Simulated extract_text (from main_app/utils.py)\ndef extract_text(file_path, file_type):\n    import docx\n    import PyPDF2\n    if file_type == '.pdf':\n        text = \"\"\n        with open(file_path, 'rb') as f:\n            reader = PyPDF2.PdfReader(f)\n            for page in reader.pages:\n                text += page.extract_text() or \"\"\n        return text\n    elif file_type in ['.doc', '.docx']:\n        doc = docx.Document(file_path)\n        return \"\\n\".join([para.text for para in doc.paragraphs])\n    elif file_type in ['.txt']:\n        with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n            return f.read()\n    else:\n        return \"\"\n\n# Simulated summarize_text (from main_app/utils.py)\ndef summarize_text(text):\n    # Summarize in chunks if text is long\n    max_chunk = 1024\n    text = text.strip().replace('\\n', ' ')\n    # We'll mock the summarizer in tests\n    from transformers import pipeline\n    summarizer                ast.Mod: operator.mod\n                }\n                for op_type, fn in ops.items():\n                    if isinstance(op, op_type):\n                        return fn(left, TestFormulaEvaluation(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        self.user = User.objects.create(username='evaluser')\n        self.formula = Formula.objects.create(\n            user=self.user,\n            name='Simple Add',\n            expression='a + b',\n            variables={'a': 'First', 'b': 'Second'}\n        )\n        self.formula_pow = Formula.objects.create(\n            user=self.user,\n            name='Power',\n            expression='pow(a, 2)',\n            variables={'a': 'Base'}\n        )\n        self.formula_math = Formula.objects.create(\n            user=self.user,\n            name='MathFunc',\n            expression='sqrt(a)',\n            variables={'a': 'Value'}\n        )\n        self.formula_unary = Formula.objects.create(\n            user=self.user,\n            name='Unary',\n            expression='-a',\n            variables={'a': 'Value'}\n        )\n        self.formula_invalid = Formula.objects.create(\n            user=self.user,\n            name='Invalid',\n            expression='a + unknown',\n            variables={'a': 'Value'}\n        )\n\n    def safe_eval(self, expr, values):\n        import ast\n        import operator\n        allowed_names = {\n            'abs': abs,\n            'max': max,\n            'min': min,\n            'pow': pow\n        }\n        import math\n        allowed_names.update({k: getattr(math, k) for k in dir(math) if not k.startswith(\"_\")})\n        class SafeEval(ast.NodeVisitor):\n            def visit(self, node):\n                if isinstance(node, ast.Expression):\n                    return self.visit(node.body)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.BinOp):\n                    left = self.visit(node.left)\n                    right = self.visit(node.right)\n                    return self._binop(node.op, left, right)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.UnaryOp):\n                    operand = self.visit(node.operand)\n                    return self._unaryop(node.op, operand)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Call):\n                    func = self.visit(node.func)\n                    args = [self.visit(a) for a in node.args]\n                    if func in allowed_names:\n                        return allowed_names[func](*args)\n                    else:\n                        raise ValueError(\"Unsafe function call\")\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Name):\n                    if node.id in values:\n                        return values[node.id]\n                    elif node.id in allowed_names:\n                        return node.id\n                    else:\n                        raise ValueError(f\"Unknown variable: {node.id}\")\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Num):\n                    return node.n\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Constant):\n                    return node.value\n                else:\n                    raise ValueError(\"Unsafe expression\")\n            def _binop(self, op, left, right):\n                ops = {\n                    ast.Add: operator.add,\n                    ast.Sub: operator.sub,\n                    ast.Mult: operator.mul,\n                    ast.Div: operator.truediv,\n                    ast.Pow: operator.pow,\n                    ast.Mod: operator.mod\n                }\n                for op_type, fn in ops.items():\n                    if isinstance(op, op_type):\n                        return fn(left, right)\n                raise ValueError(\"Unsupported operator\")\n            def _unaryop(self, op, operand):\n                if isinstance(op, ast.USub):\n                    return -operand\n                elif isinstance(op, ast.UAdd):\n                    return +operand\n                else:\n                    raise ValueError(\"Unsupported unary operator\")\n        node = ast.parse(expr, mode='eval')\n        return SafeEval().visit(node)\n\n    def test_simple_add(self):\n        result = self.safe_eval(self.formula.expression, {'a': 2, 'b': 3})\n        self.assertEqual(result, 5)\n\n    def test_pow_function(self):\n        result = self.safe_eval(self.formula_pow.expression, {'a': 4})\n        self.assertEqual(result, 16)\n\n    def test_math_function(self):\n        result = self.safe_eval(self.formula_math.expression, {'a': 9})\n        self.assertEqual(result, 3)\n\n    def test_unary_operator(self):\n        result = self.safe_eval(self.formula_unary.expression, {'a': 5})\n        self.assertEqual(result, -5)\n\n    def test_invalid_variable(self):\n        with self.assertRaises(ValueError) as cm:\n with self.assertRaises(ValueError):\n            self.safe_eval(expr, {})\n\n    def test_division_by_zero(self):\n        expr = 'a / b'\n        with self.assertRaises(ZeroDivisionError):\n =======================\nfrom django.db import models\nfrom django.contrib.auth.models import User\n\nclass Document(models.Model):\n    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)\n    file = models.FileField(upload_to='documents/')\n    uploaded_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)\n    summary = models.TextField(blank=True)\n\n    def __str__(self):\n        return self.file.name\n\nclass Formula(models.Model):\n    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)\n    name = models.CharField(max_length=100)\n    expression = models.TextField()  # The formula as a string\n    variables = models.JSONField(default=dict)  # {\"var1\": \"Description\", ...}\n    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)\n\n    def __str__(self):\n        return self.name\n\n# =======================\n# main_app/forms.py\n# =======================\nfrom django import forms\nfrom .models import Document, Formula\n\nclass DocumentUploadForm(forms.Form):\n    files = forms.FileField(widget=forms.ClearableFileInput(attrs={'multiple': True}), required=True)\n\nclass FormulaForm(forms.ModelForm):\n    class Meta:\n        model = Formula\n        fields = ['name', 'expression', 'variables']\n        widgets = {\n            'variables': forms.Textarea(attrs={'rows': 2, 'placeholder': 'JSON: {\"var1\": \"desc\", ...}'}),\n        }\n\n# =======================\n# main_app/utils.py\n# =======================\nimport os\nimport docx\nimport PyPDF2\n\nfrom transformers import pipeline\n\n# Load summarization pipeline once\nsummarizer = pipeline(\"summarization\", model=\"facebook/bart-large-cnn\")\n\ndef extract_text(file_path, file_type):\n    if file_type == '.pdf':\n        text = \"\"\n        with open(file_path, 'rb') as f:\n            reader = PyPDF2.PdfReader(f)\n            for page in reader.pages:\n                text += page.extract_text() or \"\"\n        return text\n    elif file_type in ['.doc', '.docx']:\n        doc = docx.Document(file_path)\n        return \"\\n\".join([para.text for para in doc.paragraphs])\n    elif file_type in ['.txt']:\n        with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n            return f.read()\n    else:\n        return \"\"\n\ndef summarize_text(text):\n    # Summarize in chunks if text is long\n    max_chunk = 1024\n    text = text.strip().replace('\\n', ' ')\n    if len(text) <= max_chunk:\n        summary = summarizer(text, max_length=130, min_length=30, do_sample=False)[0]['summary_text']\n        return summary\n    else:\n        chunks = [text[i:i+max_chunk] for i in range(0, len(text), max_chunk)]\n        summaries = []\n        for chunk in chunks:\n            s = summarizer(chunk, max_length=130, min_length=30, do_sample=False)[0]['summary_text']\n            summaries.append(s)\n        return \" \".join(summaries)\n\n# =======================\n# main_app/views.py\n# =======================\nfrom django.shortcuts import render, redirect\nfrom django.contrib.auth.decorators import login_required\nfrom django.contrib import messages\nfrom .forms import DocumentUploadForm, FormulaForm\nfrom .models import Document, Formula\nfrom .utils import extract_text, summarize_text\nimport os\n\n@login_required\ndef upload_documents(request):\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        form = DocumentUploadForm(request.POST, request.FILES)\n        files = request.FILES.getlist('files')\n        if form.is_valid():\n            for f in files:\n                ext = os.path.splitext(f.name)[1].lower()\n                if ext not in ['.pdf', '.doc', '.docx', '.txt']:\n                    messages.error(request, f\"Unsupported file type: {f.name}\")\n                    continue\n                doc = Document.objects.create(user=request.user, file=f)\n                doc_path = doc.file.path\n                text = extract_text(doc_path, ext)\n                if not text.strip():\n                    doc.summary = \"No extractable text found.\"\n                else:\n                    try:\n                        doc.summary = summarize_text(text)\n                    except Exception as e:\n                        doc.summary = f\"Error during summarization: {e}\"\n                doc.save()\n            messages.success(request, \"Files uploaded and summarized.\")\n            return redirect('upload_documents')\n    else:\n        form = DocumentUploadForm()\n    documents = Document.objects.filter(user=request.user).order_by('-uploaded_at')\n    return render(request, 'upload.html', {'form': form, 'documents': documents})\n\n@login_required\ndef formula_builder(request):\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        form = FormulaForm(request.POST)\n        if form.is_valid():\n            formula = form.save(commit=False)\n            formula.user = request.user\n            formula.save()\n            messages.success(request, \"Formula saved!\")\n            return redirect('formula_builder')\n    else:\n        form = FormulaForm()\n    formulas = Formula.objects.filter(user=request.user)\n    return render(request, 'formula_builder.html', {'form': form, 'formulas': formulas})\n\n@login_required\ndef evaluate_formula(request):\n    import ast\n    import operator\n\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        formula_id = request.POST.get('formula_id')\n        formula = Formula.objects.get(id=formula_id, user=request.user)\n        variables = formula.variables\n        values = {}\n        for var in variables.keys():\n            values[var] = float(request.POST.get(var, 0))\n        # Safe eval: only math operators\n        allowed_names = {\n            'abs': abs,\n            'max': max,\n            'min': min,\n            'pow': pow\n        }\n        import math\n        allowed_names.update({k: getattr(math, k) for k in dir(math) if not k.startswith(\"_\")})\n        class SafeEval(ast.NodeVisitor):\n            def visit(self, node):\n                if isinstance(node, ast.Expression):\n                    return self.visit(node.body)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.BinOp):\n                    left = self.visit(node.left)\n                    right = self.visit(node.right)\n                    return self._binop(node.op, left, right)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.UnaryOp):\n                    operand = self.visit(node.operand)\n                    return self._unaryop(node.op, operand)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Call):\n                    func = self.visit(node.func)\n                    args = [self.visit(a) for a in node.args]\n                    if func in allowed_names:\n                        return allowed_names[func](*args)\n                    else:\n                        raise ValueError(\"Unsafe function call\")\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Name):\n                    if node.id in values:\n                        return values[node.id]\n                    elif node.id in allowed_names:\n                        return node.id\n                    else:\n                        raise ValueError(f\"Unknown variable: {node.id}\")\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Num):\n                    return node.n\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Constant):\n                    return node.value\n                else:\n                    raise ValueError(\"Unsafe expression\")\n            def _binop(self, op, left, right):\n                ops = {\n                    ast.Add: operator.add,\n                    ast.Sub: operator.sub,\n                    ast.Mult: operator.mul,\n                    ast.Div: operator.truediv,\n                    ast.Pow: operator.pow,\n                    ast.Mod: operator.mod\n                }\n                for op_type, fn in ops.items():\n                    if isinstance(op, op_type):\n                        return fn(left, right)\n                raise ValueError(\"Unsupported operator\")\n            def _unaryop(self, op, operand):\n                if isinstance(op, ast.USub):\n                    return -operand\n                elif isinstance(op, ast.UAdd):\n                    return +operand\n                else:\n                    raise ValueError(\"Unsupported unary operator\")\n        try:\n            node = ast.parse(formula.expression, mode='eval')\n            result = SafeEval().visit(node)\n            messages.success(request, f\"Result: {result}\")\n        except Exception as e:\n            messages.error(request, f\"Error evaluating formula: {e}\")\n        return redirect('formula_builder')\n    return redirect('formula_builder')\n\n# =======================\n# main_app/urls.py\n# Formula.objects.get(id=formula_id, user=request.user)\n        variables = formula.variables\n        values = {}\n        for var in variables.keys():\n            values[var] = float(request.POST.get(var, 0))\n        # Safe eval: only math operators\n        allowed_names = {\n            'abs': abs,\n            'max': max,\n            'min': min,\n            'pow': pow\n        }\n        import math\n        allowed_names.update({k: getattr(math, k) for k in dir(math) if not k.startswith(\"_\")})\n        class SafeEval(ast.NodeVisitor):\n            def visit(self, node):\n                if isinstance(node, ast.Expression):\n                    return self.visit(node.body)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.BinOp):\n                    left = self.visit(node.left)\n                    right = self.visit(node.right)\n                    return self._binop(node.op, left, right)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.UnaryOp):\n 'max': max,\n            'min': min,\n            'pow': pow\n        }\n        allowed_names.update({k: getattr(math, k) for k in dir(math) if not k.startswith(\"_\")})\n        class SafeEval(ast.NodeVisitor):\n            def visit(self, node):\n                if isinstance(node, ast.Expression):\n                    return self.visit(node.body)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.BinOp):\n                    left = self.visit(node.left)\n                    right = self.visit(node.right)\n                    return self._binop(node.op, left, right)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.UnaryOp):\n                    operand = self.visit(node.operand)\n                    return self._unaryop(node.op, operand)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Call):\n                    func = self.visit(node.func)\n                    args = [self.visit(a) for a in node.args]\n                    if func in allowed_names:\n                        return allowed_names[func](*args)\n                    else:\n                        raise ValueError(\"Unsafe function call\")\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Name):\n                    if node.id in values:\n                        return values[node.id]\n                    elif node.id in allowed_names:\n                        return node.id\n                    else:\n                        raise ValueError(f\"Unknown variable: {node.id}\")\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Num):\n                    return node.n\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Constant):\n                    return node.value\n                else:\n                    raise ValueError(\"Unsafe expression\")\n            def _binop(self, op, left, right):\n                ops = {\n                    ast.Add: operator.add,\n                    ast.Sub: operator.sub,\n                    ast.Mult: operator.mul,\n                    ast.Div: operator.truediv,\n                    ast.Pow: operator.pow,\n                    ast.Mod: operator.mod\n                }\n                for op_type, fn in ops.items():\n                    if isinstance(op, op_type):\n                        return fn(left, right)\n                raise ValueError(\"Unsupported operator\")\n            def _unaryop(self, op, operand):\n                if isinstance(op, ast.USub):\n                    return -operand\n                elif isinstance(op, ast.UAdd):\n                    return +operand\n                else:\n                    raise ValueError(\"Unsupported unary operator\")\n        node = ast.parse(expression, mode='eval')\n        return SafeEval().visit(node)\n\n    def test_formula_eval_simple(self):\n        result = \"d\": \"D\"}\n        )\n\n    def tearDown(self):\n        Formula.objects.all().delete()\n        User.objects.all().delete()\n\n    def safe_eval(self, expression, values):\n        # Re-implement the SafeEval logic from views.py for testing\n        import ast\n        import operator\n        import math\n\n        allowed_names = {\n            'abs': abs,\n            'max': max,\n            'min': min,\n            'pow': pow\n        }\n        allowed_names.update({k: getattr(math, k) for k in dir(math) if not k.startswith(\"_\")})\n\n        class SafeEval(ast.NodeVisitor):\n            def visit(self, node):\n                if isinstance(node, ast.Expression):\n                    return self.visit(node.body)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.BinOp):\n                    left = self.visit(node.left)\n                    right = self.visit(node.right)\n                    return self._binop(node.op, left, right)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.UnaryOp):\n                    operand = self.visit(node.operand)\n                    return self._unaryop(node.op, operand)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Call):\n                    func = self.visit(node.func)\n                    args = [self.visit(a) for a in node.args]\n                    if func in allowed_names:\n                        return allowed_names[func](*args)\n                    else:\n                        raise ValueError(\"Unsafe function call\")\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Name):\n                    if node.id in values:\n                        return values[node.id]\n                    elif node.id in allowed_names:\n                        return node.id\n                    else:\n                        raise ValueError(f\"Unknown variable: {node.id}\")\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Num):\n                    return node.n\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Constant):\n                    return node.value\n                else:\n                    raise ValueError(\"Unsafe expression\")\n            def _binop(self, op, left, right):\n                ops = {\n                    ast.Add: operator.add,\n                    ast.Sub: operator.sub,\n                    ast.Mult: operator.mul,\n                    ast.Div: operator.truediv,\n                    ast.Pow: operator.pow,\n                    ast.Mod: operator.mod\n                }\n                for op_type, fn in ops.items():\n                    if isinstance(op, op_type):\n                        return fn(left, right)\n                raise ValueError(\"Unsupported operator\")\n            def _unaryop(self, op, operand):\n                if isinstance(op, ast.USub):\n                    return -operand\n                elif isinstance(op, ast.UAdd):\n                    return +operand\n                else:\n                    raise ValueError(\"Unsupported unary operator\")\n        node = ast.parse(expression, mode='eval')\n        return SafeEval().visit(node)\n\n    def test_simple_eval(self):\n        formula = Formula.objects.create(\n            user=self.user,\n            name=\"Sum\",\n            expression=\"x + y\",\n            variables={\"x\": \"X\", \"y\": \"Y\"}\n        )\n        result = self.safe_eval(formula.expression, {\"x\": 2, \"y\": 3})\n        self.assertEqual(result, 5)\n\n    def test_complex_eval(self):\n        result = self.safe_eval(self.formula.expression, {\"a\": 2, \"b\": 3, \"c\": 4, \"d\": 5})\n        self.assertEqual(result, 2 setUp(self):\n        self.user = User.objects.create_user(username='testuser', password='pass')\n        self.formula = Formula.objects.create(\n            user=self.user,\n            name='Sum',\n 'max': max,\n            'min': min,\n            'pow': pow\n        }\n        allowed_names.update({k: getattr(math, k) for k in dir(math) if not k.startswith(\"_\")})\n        class SafeEval(ast.NodeVisitor):\n            def visit(self, node):\n                if isinstance(node, ast.Expression):\n                    return self.visit(node.body)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.BinOp):\n                    left = self.visit(node.left)\n                    right = self.visit(node.right)\n                    return self._binop(node.op, left, right)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.UnaryOp):\n                    operand = self.visit(node.operand)\n                    return self._unaryop(node.op, operand)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Call):\n                    func = self.visit(node.func)\n                    args = [self.visit(a) for a in node.args]\n                    if func in allowed_names:\n                        return allowed_names[func](*args)\n                    else:\n                        raise ValueError(\"Unsafe function call\")\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Name):\n                    if node.id in values:\n                        return values[node.id]\n                    elif node.id in allowed_names:\n                        return node.id\n                    else:\n                        raise ValueError(f\"Unknown variable: {node.id}\")\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Num):\n                    return node.n\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Constant):\n                    return node.value\n                else:\n                    raise ValueError(\"Unsafe expression\")\n            def _binop(self, op, left, right):\n                ops = {\n                    ast.Add: operator.add,\n                    ast.Sub: operator.sub,\n                    ast.Mult: operator.mul,\n                    ast.Div: operator.truediv,\n                    ast.Pow: operator.pow,\n                    ast.Mod: operator.mod\n                }\n                for op_type, fn in ops.items():\n                    if isinstance(op, op_type):\n                        return fn(left, right)\n                raise ValueError(\"Unsupported operator\")\n            def _unaryop(self, op, operand):\n                if isinstance(op, ast.USub):\n                    return -operand\n                elif isinstance(op, ast.UAdd):\n                    return +operand\n                else:\n                    raise ValueError(\"Unsupported unary operator\")\n        node = ast.parse(expression, mode='eval')\n        return SafeEval().visit(node)\n\n    def test_formula_eval_simple(self):\n        result = self.safe_eval(self.formula.expression, {'a': 5, 'b': 7})\n        self.assertEqual(result, 12)\n\n    def test_formula_eval_with_math_func(self):\n        formula = Formula.objects.create(\n                         "# main_app/models.py\nfrom django.db import models\nfrom django.contrib.auth.models import User\n\nclass Document(models.Model):\n    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)\n    file = models.FileField(upload_to='documents/')\n    uploaded_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)\n    summary = models.TextField(blank=True)\n\n    def __str__(self):\n        return self.file.name\n\nclass Formula(models.Model):\n    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)\n    name = models.CharField(max_length=100)\n    expression = models.TextField()  # The formula as a string\n    variables = models.JSONField(default=dict)  # {\"var1\": \"Description\", ...}\n    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)\n\n    def __str__(self):\n        return self.name\n\n# main_app/forms.py\nfrom django import forms\nfrom .models import Formula\n\nclass DocumentUploadForm(forms.Form):\n    files = forms.FileField(widget=forms.ClearableFileInput(attrs={'multiple': True}), required=True)\n\nclass FormulaForm(forms.ModelForm):\n    class Meta:\n        model = Formula\n        fields = ['name', 'expression', 'variables']\n        widgets = {\n            'variables': forms.Textarea(attrs={'rows': 2, 'placeholder': 'JSON: {\"var1\": \"Description\", ...}'}),\n        }\n\n# main_app/utils.py\nimport os\nimport docx\nimport PyPDF2\nfrom transformers import pipeline\n\n# Load summarization pipeline once at module load\nsummarizer = pipeline(\"summarization\", model=\"facebook/bart-large-cnn\")\n\ndef extract_text(file_path, file_type):\n    \"\"\"\n    Extracts text from file given its path and extension.\n    Supports PDF, DOCX, TXT.\n    \"\"\"\n    if file_type == '.pdf':\n        text = \"\"\n        with open(file_path, 'rb') as f:\n            reader = PyPDF2.PdfReader(f)\n            for page in reader.pages:\n                text += page.extract_text() or \"\"\n        return text\n    elif file_type in ['.doc', '.docx']:\n        doc = docx.Document(file_path)\n        return \"\\n\".join([para.text for para in doc.paragraphs])\n    elif file_type in ['.txt']:\n        with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n            return f.read()\n    else:\n        return \"\"\n\ndef summarize_text(text):\n    \"\"\"\n    Uses Huggingface transformers to summarize text.\n    If text is long, splits into chunks.\n    \"\"\"\n    max_chunk = 1024\n    text = text.strip().replace('\\n', ' ')\n    if len(text) <= max_chunk:\n        summary = summarizer(text, max_length=130, min_length=30, do_sample=False)[0]['summary_text']\n        return summary\n    else:\n        chunks = [text[i:i+max_chunk] for i in range(0, len(text), max_chunk)]\n        summaries = []\n        for chunk in chunks:\n            s = summarizer(chunk, max_length=130, min_length=30, do_sample=False)[0]['summary_text']\n            summaries.append(s)\n        return \" \".join(summaries)\n\n# main_app/views.py\nfrom django.shortcuts import render, redirect\nfrom django.contrib.auth.decorators import login_required\nfrom django.contrib import messages\nfrom .forms import DocumentUploadForm, FormulaForm\nfrom .models import Document, Formula\nfrom .utils import extract_text, summarize_text\nimport os\n\n@login_required\ndef upload_documents(request):\n    \"\"\"\n    Handles document upload, extraction, and summarization.\n    \"\"\"\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        form = DocumentUploadForm(request.POST, request.FILES)\n        files = request.FILES.getlist('files')\n        if form.is_valid():\n            for f in files:\n                ext = os.path.splitext(f.name)[1].lower()\n                if ext not in ['.pdf', '.doc', '.docx', '.txt']:\n                    messages.error(request, f\"Unsupported file type: {f.name}\")\n                    continue\n                doc = Document.objects.create(user=request.user, file=f)\n                doc_path = doc.file.path\n                text = extract_text(doc_path, ext)\n                if not text.strip():\n                    doc.summary = \"No extractable text found.\"\n                else:\n                    try:\n                        doc.summary = summarize_text(text)\n                    except Exception as e:\n                        doc.summary = f\"Error during summarization: {e}\"\n                doc.save()\n            messages.success(request, \"Files uploaded and summarized.\")\n            return redirect('upload_documents')\n    else:\n        form = DocumentUploadForm()\n    documents = Document.objects.filter(user=request.user).order_by('-uploaded_at')\n    return render(request, 'upload.html', {'form': form, 'documents': documents})\n\n@login_required\ndef formula_builder(request):\n    \"\"\"\n    Formula builder view for creating and listing formulas.\n    \"\"\"\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        form = FormulaForm(request.POST)\n        if form.is_valid():\n            formula = form.save(commit=False)\n            formula.user = request.user\n            formula.save()\n            messages.success(request, \"Formula saved!\")\n            return redirect('formula_builder')\n    else:\n        form = FormulaForm()\n    formulas = Formula.objects.filter(user=request.user)\n    return render(request, 'formula_builder.html', {'form': form, 'formulas': formulas})\n\n@login_required\ndef evaluate_formula(request):\n    \"\"\"\n    Evaluates a formula with user-provided variables.\n    Safe evaluation using AST.\n    \"\"\"\n    import ast\n    import operator\n\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        formula_id = request.POST.get('formula_id')\n        formula = Formula.objects.get(id=formula_id, user=request.user)\n        variables = formula.variables\n        values = {}\n        for var in variables.keys():\n            try:\n                values[var] = float(request.POST.get(var, 0))\n            except ValueError:\n                messages.error(request, f\"Invalid value for {var}\")\n                return redirect('formula_builder')\n        # Safe eval: only math operators\n        allowed_names = {\n            'abs': abs,\n            'max': max,\n            'min': min,\n            'pow': pow\n        }\n        import math\n        allowed_names.update({k: getattr(math, k) for k in dir(math) if not k.startswith(\"_\")})\n        class SafeEval(ast.NodeVisitor):\n            def visit(self, node):\n                if isinstance(node, ast.Expression):\n                    return self.visit(node.body)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.BinOp):\n                    left = self.visit(node.left)\n                    right = self.visit(node.right)\n                    return self._binop(node.op, left, right)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.UnaryOp):\n                    operand = self.visit(node.operand)\n                    return self._unaryop(node.op, operand)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Call):\n                    func = self.visit(node.func)\n                    args = [self.visit(a) for a in node.args]\n                    if func in allowed_names:\n                        return allowed_names[func](*args)\n                    else:\n                        raise ValueError(\"Unsafe function call\")\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Name):\n                    if node.id in values:\n                        return values[node.id]\n                    elif node.id in allowed_names:\n                        return node.id\n                    else:\n                        raise ValueError(f\"Unknown variable: {node.id}\")\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Num):\n                    return node.n\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Constant):\n                    return node.value\n                else:\n                    raise ValueError(\"Unsafe expression\")\n            def _binop(self, op, left, right):\n                ops = {\n                    ast.Add: operator.add,\n                    ast.Sub: operator.sub,\n                    ast.Mult: operator.mul,\n                    ast.Div: operator.truediv,\n                    ast.Pow: operator.pow,\n                    ast.Mod: operator.mod\n                }\n                for op_type, fn in ops.items():\n                    if isinstance(op, op_type):\n                        return fn(left, right)\n                raise ValueError(\"Unsupported operator\")\n            def _unaryop(self, op, operand):\n                if isinstance(op, ast.USub):\n                    return -operand\n                elif isinstance(op, ast.UAdd):\n                    return +operand\n                else:\n                    raise ValueError(\"Unsupported unary operator\")\n        try:\n            node = ast.parse(formula.expression, mode='eval')\n            result = SafeEval().visit(node)\n            messages.success(request, f\"Result: {result}\")\n        except Exception as e:\n            messages.error(request, f\"Error evaluating formula: {e}\")\n        return redirect('formula_builder')\n    return redirect('formula_builder')\n\n# main_app/urls.py\nfrom django.urls import path\nfrom . import views\n\nurlpatterns = [\n    path('upload/', views.upload_documents, name='upload_documents'),\n    path('formulas/', views.formula_builder, name='formula_builder'),\n    path('evaluate_formula/', views.evaluate_formula, name='evaluate_formula'),\n]\n\n# import ast\n    import operator\n\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        formula_id = request.POST.get('formula_id')\n        formula = Formula.objects.get(id=formula_id, user=request.user)\n        variables = formula.variables\n        values = {}\n        for var in variables.keys():\n            try:\n                values[var] = float(request.POST.get(var, 0))\n            except ValueError:\n                messages.error(request, f\"Invalid value for {var}\")\n                return redirect('formula_builder')\n        # Safe eval: only math operators\n        allowed_names = {\n            'abs': abs,\n            'max': max,\n            'min': min,\n            'pow': pow\n        }\n        import math\n        allowed_names.update({k: getattr(math, k) for k in dir(math) if not k.startswith(\"_\")})\n        class SafeEval(ast.NodeVisitor):\n            def visit(self, node):\n                if isinstance(node, ast.Expression):\n                    return self.visit(node.body)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.BinOp):\n                    left = self.visit(node.left)\n                    right = self.visit(node.right)\n                    return self._binop(node.op, left, right)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.UnaryOp):\n                    operand = self.visit(node.operand)\n                    return self._unaryop(node.op, operand)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Call):\n                    func = self.visit(node.func)\n                    args = [self.visit(a) for a in node.args]\n                    if func in allowed_names:\n                        return allowed_names[func](*args)\n                    else:\n                        raise ValueError(\"Unsafe function call\")\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Name):\n                    if node.id in values:\n                        return values[node.id]\n                    elif node.id in allowed_names:\n                        return node.id\n                    else:\n                        raise ValueError(f\"Unknown variable: {node.id}\")\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Num):\n                    return node.n\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Constant):\n                    return node.value\n                else:\n                    raise ValueError(\"Unsafe expression\")\n            def _binop(self, op, left, right):\n                ops = {\n                    ast.Add: operator.add,\n                    ast.Sub: operator.sub,\n                    ast.Mult: operator.mul,\n                    ast.Div: operator.truediv,\n                    ast.Pow: operator.pow,\n                    ast.Mod: operator.mod\n                }\n                for op_type, fn in ops.items():\n                    if isinstance(op, op_type):\n                        return fn(left, right)\n                raise ValueError(\"Unsupported operator\")\n            def _unaryop(self, op, operand):\n                if isinstance(op, ast.USub):\n                    return -operand\n                elif isinstance(op, ast.UAdd):\n                    return +operand\n                else:\n                    raise ValueError(\"Unsupported unary operator\")\n        try:\n            node = ast.parse(formula.expression, mode='eval')\n            result = SafeEval().visit(node)\n            messages.success(request, f\"Result: {result}\")\n        except Exception as e:\n            messages.error(request, f\"Error evaluating formula: {e}\")\n        return redirect('formula_builder')\n    return redirect('formula_builder')\n\n# main_app/urls.py\nfrom django.urls import path\nfrom . import views\n\nurlpatterns = [\n    path('upload/', views.upload_documents,    \"\"\"\n    Uses Huggingface transformers to summarize text.\n    If text is long, splits into chunks.\n    \"\"\"\n    max_chunk = 1024\n    text = text.strip().replace('\\n', ' ')\n    if len(text) <= max_chunk:\n        summary = summarizer(text, max_length=130, min_length=30, do_sample=False)[0]['summary_text']\n        return summary\n    else:\n        chunks = [text[i:i+max_chunk]                 except Exception as e:\n                        doc.summary = f\"Error during summarization: {e}\"\n                doc.save()\n            messages.success(request, \"Files uploaded Document.objects.filter(user=request.user).order_by('-uploaded_at')\n    return render(request, 'upload.html', {'form': form, 'documents': documents})\n\n@login_required\ndef formula_builder(request):\n    \"\"\"\n    Formula builder view for creating and listing formulas.\n    \"\"\"\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        form = FormulaForm(request.POST)\n        if form.is_valid():\n            formula = form.save(commit=False)\n            formula.user = request.user\n            formula.save()\n            messages.success(request, \"Formula saved!\")\n            return redirect('formula_builder')\n    else:\n        form = FormulaForm()\n    formulas = Formula.objects.filter(user=request.user)\n    return render(request, 'formula_builder.html', {'form': form, 'formulas': formulas})\n\n@login_required\ndef evaluate_formula(request):\n    \"\"\"\n    Evaluates a formula with user-provided variables.\n    Safe evaluation using AST.\n    \"\"\"\n    import ast\n    import operator\n\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        formula_id = request.POST.get('formula_id')\n        formula = Formula.objects.get(id=formula_id, user=request.user)\n        variables = formula.variables\n        values = {}\n        for var in variables.keys():\n            try:\n                values[var] = float(request.POST.get(var, 0))\n            except ValueError:\n                messages.error(request, f\"Invalid value for {var}\")\n                return redirect('formula_builder')\n        # Safe eval: only math operators\n        allowed_names = {\n            'abs': abs,\n            'max': max,\n            'min': min,\n            'pow': pow\n        }\n        import math\n        allowed_names.update({k: getattr(math, k) for k in dir(math) if not k.startswith(\"_\")})\n        class SafeEval(ast.NodeVisitor):\n            def visit(self, node):\n                if isinstance(node, ast.Expression):\n                    return self.visit(node.body)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.BinOp):\n                    left = self.visit(node.left)\n                    right = self.visit(node.right)\n                    return self._binop(node.op, left, right)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.UnaryOp):\n                    operand = self.visit(node.operand)\n                    return self._unaryop(node.op, operand)\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Call):\n                    func = self.visit(node.func)\n                    args = [self.visit(a) for a in node.args]\n                    if func in allowed_names:\n                        return allowed_names[func](*args)\n                    else:\n                        raise ValueError(\"Unsafe function call\")\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Name):\n                    if node.id in values:\n                        return values[node.id]\n                    elif node.id in allowed_names:\n                        return node.id\n                    else:\n                        raise ValueError(f\"Unknown variable: {node.id}\")\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Num):\n                    return node.n\n                elif isinstance(node, ast.Constant):\n                    return node.value\n                else:\n                    raise ValueError(\"Unsafe expression\")\n            def _binop(self, op, left, right):\n                ops = {\n                    ast.Add: operator.add,\n                    ast.Sub: operator.sub,\n                    ast.Mult: operator.mul,\n                    ast.Div: operator.truediv,\n                    ast.Pow: operator.pow,\n                    ast.Mod: operator.mod\n                }\n                for op_type, fn in ops.items():\n                    if isinstance(op, op_type):\n                        return fn(left, right)\n                raise ValueError(\"Unsupported operator\")\n            def _unaryop(self, op, operand):\n                if isinstance(op, ast.USub):\n                    return -operand\n                elif isinstance(op, ast.UAdd):\n                    return +operand\n                else:\n                    raise ValueError(\"Unsupported unary operator\")\n        try:\n            node = ast.parse(formula.expression, mode='eval')\n            result = SafeEval().visit(node)\n            messages.success(request, f\"Result: {result}\")\n        except Exception as e:\n            messages.error(request, f\"Error evaluating formula: {e}\")\n        return redirect('formula_builder')\n    return redirect('formula_builder')\n\n# main_app/urls.py\nfrom django.urls import path\nfrom . import views\n\nurlpatterns = [\n    path('upload/', views.upload_documents,
